\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__qmc_8py_source_l02478}02478\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ Lloyd-\/Max\ algorithm\ is\ an\ iterative\ process\ with\ the\ purpose\ of\ improving}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__qmc_8py_source_l02479}02479\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ the\ dispersion\ of\ samples.\ For\ given\ sample:\ (i)\ compute\ a\ Voronoi}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__qmc_8py_source_l02480}02480\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ Tessellation;\ (ii)\ find\ the\ centroid\ of\ each\ Voronoi\ cell;\ (iii)\ move\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__qmc_8py_source_l02481}02481\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ samples\ toward\ the\ centroid\ of\ their\ respective\ cell.\ See\ [1]\_,\ [2]\_.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__qmc_8py_source_l02482}02482\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__qmc_8py_source_l02483}02483\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ A\ relaxation\ factor\ is\ used\ to\ control\ how\ fast\ samples\ can\ move\ at\ each}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__qmc_8py_source_l02484}02484\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ iteration.\ This\ factor\ is\ starting\ at\ 2\ and\ ending\ at\ 1\ after\ \`{}maxiter\`{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__qmc_8py_source_l02485}02485\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ following\ an\ exponential\ decay.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__qmc_8py_source_l02486}02486\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__qmc_8py_source_l02487}02487\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ The\ process\ converges\ to\ equally\ spaced\ samples.\ It\ implies\ that\ measures}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__qmc_8py_source_l02488}02488\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ like\ the\ discrepancy\ could\ suffer\ from\ too\ many\ iterations.\ On\ the\ other}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__qmc_8py_source_l02489}02489\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ hand,\ L1\ and\ L2\ distances\ should\ improve.\ This\ is\ especially\ true\ with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__qmc_8py_source_l02490}02490\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ QMC\ methods\ which\ tend\ to\ favor\ the\ discrepancy\ over\ other\ criteria.}}
